#################################
######## THE LONGBEARDS #########
#################################
			
### In order: 				
#		
# Line of Durin
# line of Delingur "keepers of thorin's halls"
# Line of Wegdrasil Longbeard inhabitants of Tumnogoth Iaur
# Line of Uni merchants of the river Lhun. Guardians of the river waystation of Kheledul
# Line of Hor Longbeard colonists of the northern blue mountains
# Line of Gorin (Nordinbad) Guardians of Azan-zaram
# House Silverbeard - One time rulers of Fireheart Mine
# Line of Theklel
# Other Longbeards:
# Line of Stiling ~ Disgraced former rulers of Fuhmdusha, exiled during the Angmar start date
# Line of Viglund ~ maintained a small waystation at Erebor during the early third age
# Line of Grúni ~ Lords of Azanulibar-dûm before the Fall of Khazad-dum
# Line of Bori ~ Minor clan at the northern edge of the Iron Hills, dies out after the Angmar start date 
# Line of Mardin ~ Lords of the East-gate of Moria and Azalnulbizar
# Line of Grósi ~ Tenders of the central Mines of Zirakzigil
# Line of Thórak - Keepers of the West-gate of Khazad-dum
# Line of Drár - Stewards of the Hall of a Thousand Pillars
# Line of Mithúr ~ Chief Miners of Caradhras (Dukes)
# Line of Marin ~ Vassal lords in the duchy of Barazinbar
# Line of Brogur ~ Vassal lords in the duchy of Barazinbar
# Line of Frólni ~ High Lords of the Bundushathûr, Vassals of Khazad-dûm
# Line of Brogni ~ Vassal lords in the Bundushathûr
# Line of Samar ~ Vassal lords in the Bundushathûr
# Line of Sogin ~ Vassal lords in Fuhmdusha, die out during the Last Alliance

##########################
### The Line of Durin ####
##########################

lineofdurin1 = { # Durin the Deathless
    name = Durin
    dynasty = dynasty_durin			
    religion = faith_khazad			
    culture = longbeards
	dna = durin_dna

    sexuality = heterosexual

    trait = education_stewardship_5

    trait = diligent 
    trait = generous
    trait = just

    trait = intellect_good_3
    trait = poet
	trait = dwarf_father

    2.2.4 = {		
        birth = yes
        give_nickname = nick_the_deathless
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
        }	
    }			
    412.5.12 = {
        death = { death_reason = death_natural_causes }	
    }	
}
